<h2 id="SC">SOUTH COAST</h2>
<table id="tSC" class="tabledata obs_table" summary="Observations for SC including temperature, wind, rain and other weather elements" cellspacing="0" border="1"> <!-- ABCD open product division table before col headings -->
<colgroup>

<thead>
<tr>
  <th id="tSC-station" rowspan="2" class="rowleftcolumn">&nbsp;</th>
  <th id="tSC-datetime" rowspan="2" title="Date and local time">Date/Time<br><acronym title="Eastern Daylight Savings Time">EDT</acronym></th>
  <th id="tSC-tmp" rowspan="2"><abbr title="Temperature, degrees Celsius">Temp<br>°C</abbr></th>
  <th id="tSC-apptmp" rowspan="2"><abbr title="Apparent Temperature, degrees Celsius">App<br>Temp<br>°C</abbr></th>

<thead>
<tr>
  <th id="tST-station" rowspan="2" class="rowleftcolumn">&nbsp;</th>
  <th id="tST-datetime" rowspan="2" title="Date and local time">Date/Time<br><acronym title="Eastern Daylight Savings Time">EDT</acronym></th>
  <th id="tST-tmp" rowspan="2"><abbr title="Temperature, degrees Celsius">Temp<br>°C</abbr></th>
  <th id="tST-apptmp" rowspan="2"><abbr title="Apparent Temperature, degrees Celsius">App<br>Temp<br>°C</abbr></th>
  <th id="tST-dewpoint" rowspan="2"><abbr title="Dew Point Temperature, degrees Celsius">Dew<br>Point<br>°C</abbr></th>
  <th id="tST-relhum" rowspan="2"><abbr title="Relative Humidity, percentage">Rel<br>Hum<br>%</abbr></th>
  <th id="tST-delta-t" rowspan="2"><abbr title="Wet Bulb Depression, degrees Celsius">Delta-T<br>°C</abbr></th>
  <th id="tST-wind" colspan="5">Wind</th>
  <th id="tST-press-msl" rowspan="2"><abbr title="Pressure MSL, hectopascals">Press<br>MSL<br>hPa</abbr></th>

<!-- station information for state/territory output -->
<div class="noPrint">
        <h3>Weather station information</h3>
<ul>
<li>AWS = Automatic Weather Station</li>
<li>AgIn&nbsp; = Agricultural Institute</li>
<li>RS&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; = Research Station</li>
<li>* Apparent temperature (App Temp) for Sydney - Observatory Hill is calculated
using temperature observations collected at Sydney - Observatory Hill and
wind observations collected at Fort Denison, as wind observations are not currently provided
for Sydney - Observatory Hill.</li>
<li>Portable automatic weather stations (PAWS) are operated by other organisations, such as Fire and Emergency Services, and are included here by agreement.
Portable stations may be deployed to a location for a short period and their location may be subject to change without notice.
Wind observations from these stations are provided from heights of either three (3) or ten (10) metres above ground level (AGL).
</li>
<li>Observations are collected in the New South Wales time zone (Eastern Standard Time) which includes daylight savings in the summer period. Some locations may have a different local time, including weather stations on offshore islands or near state borders. Since 'Rain since 9am' totals and other values are based on the New South Wales time zone, they may not be displayed correctly for these locations. Observations at Coolangatta are collected in the Queensland time zone, which does not include daylight savings.</li>
</ul>


<h3 id="DataQuality">Data quality</h3>
<p>These observations have been taken from the Bureau of Meteorology's real-time system. Most are generated automatically, 
with only limited quality checks performed. It is possible for incorrect values to appear. Further information can be found at 
<a href="http://www.bom.gov.au/catalogue/observations/about-weather-observations.shtml">About Latest Weather Observations</a>. 
Please check the <a href="http://www.bom.gov.au/other/disclaimer.shtml">disclaimer</a> before using these data.</p>
</div>
